                                    DiscountSurch:=("Sales Line"."Line Discount %"*-1);
                                  END ELSE IF "Sales Line"."Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    DiscountSurch:="Sales Line"."Surcharge %";
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      CurrentDocumentType@1100409000 : ',,Pro Forma Invoice,Pro Forma Credit Memo,,,,Posted Invoice,Posted Credit Memo';
      InvoiceNo@1100409001 : Code[30];
      WageComponent@1100409002 : Record 11012014;
      WageDescr@1100409003 : Text;
      Employee@1100409004 : Record 5200;
      ProjectCostPlusEntry@1000000000 : Record 11012019;
      WageDesc@1000000001 : Text;
      DiscountSurch@1000000002 : Decimal;
      Attachfile@1100409005 : Boolean;
      Ok@1100409006 : Boolean;
      CompanyInfo@1100285100 : Record 79;
      HourComm@1100285101 : Text;

    PROCEDURE SetFilters@1100409016(InvoiceNoIn@1100409000 : Code[30];CurrentDocumentTypeIn@1100409001 : ',,Pro Forma Invoice,Pro Forma Credit Memo,,,,Posted Invoice,Posted Credit Memo');
    BEGIN
      CurrentDocumentType:=CurrentDocumentTypeIn;
      InvoiceNo:=InvoiceNoIn;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineDocumentType@1100525008();
    VAR
      SalesHeaderInv@1100525000 : Record 36;
      SalesHeaderCr@1100525001 : Record 36;
    BEGIN
      CASE TRUE OF
        "Sales Header".HASFILTER OR "Sales Header".MARKEDONLY:
          BEGIN
            SalesHeaderInv.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesHeaderInv."Document Type"::Invoice);
            SalesHeaderCr.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesHeaderCr."Document Type"::"Credit Memo");
            IF "Sales Header".GETFILTER("Document Type") = SalesHeaderInv.GETFILTER("Document Type") THEN
              CurrentDocumentType := CurrentDocumentType::"Pro Forma Invoice";
            IF "Sales Header".GETFILTER("Document Type") = SalesHeaderCr.GETFILTER("Document Type") THEN
              CurrentDocumentType := CurrentDocumentType::"Pro Forma Credit Memo";
          END;
        "Sales Invoice Header".HASFILTER OR "Sales Invoice Header".MARKEDONLY:
          BEGIN
            CurrentDocumentType := CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Invoice";
          END;
        "Sales Cr.Memo Header".HASFILTER OR "Sales Cr.Memo Header".MARKEDONLY:
          BEGIN
            CurrentDocumentType := CurrentDocumentType::"Posted Credit Memo";
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetCurrentDocType@1100409000(CurrentDocumentTypeIn@1100409000 : ',,Pro Forma Invoice,Pro Forma Credit Memo,,,,Posted Invoice,Posted Credit Memo');
    BEGIN
      CurrentDocumentType:=CurrentDocumentTypeIn;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetHourComment@1100285104(VAR ProjectCostPlusEntry@1100285100 : Record 11012019) lvHourComm : Text;
    VAR
      PostedHourLine@1100285101 : Record 11012085;
      ProjectCostPlusEntry2@1100285102 : Record 11012019;
      HourAccountingCommentLine@1100285103 : Record 11128234;
      text1@1100285104 : Text;
      text2@1100285105 : Text;
      maxLen@1100285106 : Integer;
      HourLine@1100583000 : Record 11012039;
      OpenHour@1100285107 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      //>>190305
      lvHourComm := '';
      OpenHour := FALSE;
      //>>190314
      // maxLen := MAXSTRLEN(HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment);
      // IF MAXSTRLEN(PostedHourLine.Comment) < maxLen THEN
      //  maxLen := MAXSTRLEN(PostedHourLine.Comment);
      maxLen := 50;
      //<<190314

      ProjectCostPlusEntry2.COPYFILTERS(ProjectCostPlusEntry);
      ProjectCostPlusEntry2.SETRANGE("Posted Hour Year",1,9999);
      ProjectCostPlusEntry2.SETRANGE("Posted Hour Week",1,54);
      IF ProjectCostPlusEntry2.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
        ProjectCostPlusEntry2.CALCFIELDS("Cost Type");
        IF ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Cost Type"=ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Cost Type"::Labor THEN BEGIN
          PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Employee No.",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Employee No.");
          PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Year,ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Posted Hour Year");
          PostedHourLine.SETRANGE(Week,ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Posted Hour Week");
          PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Line No.",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Posted Hour Line No.");
      //    PostedHourLine.SETFILTER(Comment,'<>%1','');
          IF PostedHourLine.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
      //>>190314
      //      lvHourComm += PostedHourLine.Comment;
            HourAccountingCommentLine.SETRANGE("Table Name",HourAccountingCommentLine."Table Name"::"Posted Hour Line");
            HourAccountingCommentLine.SETRANGE("Record ID",PostedHourLine.RECORDID);
            IF HourAccountingCommentLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              text1 := COPYSTR(PostedHourLine.Comment,1,maxLen-3);
              text2 := COPYSTR(HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment,1,STRLEN(text1));
              IF text1 <> text2 THEN
                lvHourComm += PostedHourLine.Comment;
            END;
            IF HourAccountingCommentLine.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
              lvHourComm += HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment;
            UNTIL HourAccountingCommentLine.NEXT=0
            ELSE
              lvHourComm += PostedHourLine.Comment;

      //<<190314
          UNTIL PostedHourLine.NEXT=0;
        END;
      UNTIL ProjectCostPlusEntry2.NEXT=0;
      //<<190305

      //>> 200214
      IF lvHourComm<>'' THEN
        EXIT(lvHourComm);
      //<<

      //>> 200117 ORANGO.SB RFC1256 #27325 Get comment for open hours
      ProjectCostPlusEntry2.COPYFILTERS(ProjectCostPlusEntry);
      IF ProjectCostPlusEntry2.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
        ProjectCostPlusEntry2.CALCFIELDS("Cost Type");
        IF ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Cost Type"=ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Cost Type"::Labor THEN BEGIN
          HourLine.SETRANGE("Employee No.",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Employee No.");
          HourLine.SETRANGE("Wage Component",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Wage Component");
          HourLine.SETRANGE("Project No.",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Project No.");
          HourLine.SETRANGE("Cost Object",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Cost Object");
          IF HourLine.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              IF HourLine.GetExecutionDate() = ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Execution Date" THEN BEGIN
                OpenHour:= TRUE;
                HourAccountingCommentLine.SETRANGE("Table Name",HourAccountingCommentLine."Table Name"::"Hour Accounting Line");
                HourAccountingCommentLine.SETRANGE("Record ID",HourLine.RECORDID);
                IF HourAccountingCommentLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                  text1 := COPYSTR(HourLine.Comment,1,maxLen-3);
                  text2 := COPYSTR(HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment,1,STRLEN(text1));
                  IF text1 <> text2 THEN
                    lvHourComm += HourLine.Comment;
                END;
                IF HourAccountingCommentLine.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
                  lvHourComm += HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment;
                UNTIL HourAccountingCommentLine.NEXT=0
                ELSE
                  lvHourComm += HourLine.Comment;
              END;
            UNTIL HourLine.NEXT=0;
          END;// ELSE BEGIN
          //>> 200214
          IF NOT OpenHour THEN BEGIN
            CLEAR(PostedHourLine);
            PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Employee No.",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Employee No.");
            PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Wage Component",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Wage Component");
            PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Project No.",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Project No.");
            PostedHourLine.SETRANGE("Cost Object",ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Cost Object");
            IF PostedHourLine.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN
              REPEAT
                IF PostedHourLine.GetExecutionDate() = ProjectCostPlusEntry2."Execution Date" THEN BEGIN
                  HourAccountingCommentLine.SETRANGE("Table Name",HourAccountingCommentLine."Table Name"::"Posted Hour Line");
                  HourAccountingCommentLine.SETRANGE("Record ID",PostedHourLine.RECORDID);
                  IF HourAccountingCommentLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                    text1 := COPYSTR(PostedHourLine.Comment,1,maxLen-3);
                    text2 := COPYSTR(HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment,1,STRLEN(text1));
                    IF text1 <> text2 THEN
                      lvHourComm += PostedHourLine.Comment;
                  END;
                  IF HourAccountingCommentLine.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT
                    lvHourComm += HourAccountingCommentLine.Comment;
                  UNTIL HourAccountingCommentLine.NEXT=0
                  ELSE
                    lvHourComm += PostedHourLine.Comment;
                END;
              UNTIL PostedHourLine.NEXT=0;
            END;

          //<<
        END;
      UNTIL ProjectCostPlusEntry2.NEXT=0;
      //<<
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      190305 ORANGO.DL RFC1171 copy of report 81667 and added comments from posted hourlines
      200117 ORANGO.SB RFC1256 #27325 Get comment for open hours
      200214 ORANGO.SB RFC1256 #27325 Get comment for hours generated when open but then was posted
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
